!(import! &self MinerMatch.metta)

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/miner/MinerMatchTest.metta.answers',

;; Load sample data
;; ### Algorithm Sketch
; Given a collection of data trees T, a minimum support ms and an
; initial collection of patterns Candidate (containing at least the identity
; pattern, the pattern mining algorithm works as follows
; 1. Select a pattern P from C
; 2. Extract the valuation set of P over T, called V
; 3. Determine the shallow abstractions of V, called A
; 4. Specialize P by composing it with elements in A
; 5. Add the resulting specializations with enough support in C,
;    discard the others
; 6. Repeat till termination
;; Import utils
!(import! &self MinerUtils.metta)

%~ load_answer_file( '/opt/logicmoo_workspace/packs_sys/logicmoo_opencog/MeTTa/vspace-metta/examples/compat/miner/MinerMatchTest.metta.answers',

;; Tuple count grounded python function
; !(extend-py! helper)
;; This is very slow, use the grounded python function instead
;;; Collection of functions operating on numbers
;; Define max
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,max,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: max 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[max,X,Y],[if,[>,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (max $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (> $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Define min
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,min,[->,A,A,A]])
  (: min 
    (-> $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[min,X,Y],[if,[<,X,Y],X,Y])
  (= 
    (min $X $Y) 
    (if 
      (< $X $Y) $X $Y))


;; Clamp a number to be within a certain range
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,clamp,[->,A,A,A,A]])
  (: clamp 
    (-> $A $A $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[clamp,X,L,U],[max,L,[min,U,X]])
  (= 
    (clamp $X $L $U) 
    (max $L 
      (min $U $X)))


;; Define abs
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,abs,[->,A,A]])
  (: abs 
    (-> $A $A))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[abs,X],[if,[<,X,0],[*,-1,X],X])
  (= 
    (abs $X) 
    (if 
      (< $X 0) 
      (* -1 $X) $X))


;; Define <=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,<=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: <= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[<=,X,Y],[or,[<,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (<= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (< $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define >=
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,>=,[->,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: >= 
    (-> $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[>=,X,Y],[or,[>,X,Y],[==,X,Y]])
  (= 
    (>= $X $Y) 
    (or 
      (> $X $Y) 
      (== $X $Y)))


;; Define approximately equal
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,approxEq,[->,A,A,A,'Bool']])
  (: approxEq 
    (-> $A $A $A Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[approxEq,X,Y,Epsilon],[<=,[abs,[-,X,Y]],Epsilon])
  (= 
    (approxEq $X $Y $Epsilon) 
    (<= 
      (abs 
        (- $X $Y)) $Epsilon))

    (-> Nat Nat))

;; Define a generic less than operator, â©», for Nat.  < cannot be used
;; because it is a built-in, its type is hardwired and cannot be
;; overloaded.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'â©»',[->,'Nat','Nat','Bool']])
  (: â©» 
    (-> Nat Nat Bool))


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['â©»',_,'Z'],'False')
  (= 
    (â©» $_ Z) False)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['â©»','Z',['S',_]],'True')
  (= 
    (â©» Z 
      (S $_)) True)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['â©»',['S',X],['S',Y]],['â©»',X,Y])

    (â©» 
      (S $X) 
      (S $Y)) 
    (â©» $X $Y))


;; Overload â©» for Number.

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['â©»',X,Y],[<,X,Y])

;; Return the ceiling of a non negative number.  If the number is

  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,ceil,[->,'Number','Number']])

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[ceil,N],[fromNat,[fromNumber,N]])

    (ceil $N) 
    (fromNat 
      (fromNumber $N)))


;; Convert Number to Bool.  Anything above 0 converts to True.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'number->bool',[->,'Number','Bool']])
  (: number->bool

;; Convert Bool to Number.  False converts to 0, True converts to 1.
  ; Action: load=metta_atom('&self',[:,'bool->number',[->,'Bool','Number']])

  (= 
    (bool->number False) 0)


  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['bool->number','True'],1)
  (= 
    (bool->number True) 1)

;; Collects unique valuation sets.
;; A work around to put valuations to a different space
;; unfortunately we still don't have a way to call
;; a function in another (not &self) space
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['new-named-space',Name],[let,Space,['new-space'],['add-atom','&self',[=,['named-space',Name],Space]]])
  (= 
    (new-named-space $Name) 
    (let $Space 
      (new-space) 
      (add-atom &self 
        (= 
          (named-space $Name) $Space))))

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[count,Pattern,Dbspace,Xvar,Yvar],[let,Result,[let,Var,[getvar,Pattern,Xvar,Yvar],[if,[==,Var,'None'],[],[collapse,[match,Dbspace,Pattern,Var]]]],['TupleCount',Result]])

;; iSurprisingness formula

  (= 
    (isurprisingness $Pattern $Dbspace) 
    (case $Pattern 
      ( ( (candidate 
            (and $P1 $P2) $Cnt)

                  (count $P1 $Dbspace $Xvar $Yvar))) 
              ($Pp2 
                (prob 
                  (count $P2 $Dbspace $Xvar $Yvar))) 
              ($P1p2 
                (* $Pp1 $Pp2)) 
              ($P 
                (prob $Cnt))) 
            (/ 
              (max 
                (- $P $P1p2) 
                (- $P1p2 $P)) $P))) 
        ( (candidate 
            (and $P1 $P2 $P3) $Cnt) 
          (let* 
            ( ($Pp1 
                (prob 
                  (count $P1 $Dbspace $Xvar $Yvar))) 
              ($Pp2 
                (prob 
                  (count $P2 $Dbspace $Xvar $Yvar))) 
              ($Pp3

              ($Pp1p3

                    (and $P1 $P3) $Dbspace $Xvar $Yvar)))

  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',['Candidate',['S',K],LinkType,Dbspace,Minsup,Xvar,Yvar],['let*',[[Prev,[if,[==,K,'Z'],'Z',[fromNumber,[-,[fromNat,K],1]]]],[Comb,[',',[get_pattern,['Candidate',K,LinkType,Dbspace,Minsup,Xvar,Yvar]],[get_pattern,['Candidate',Prev,LinkType,Dbspace,Minsup,Xvar,Yvar]]]]],[support,Comb,Dbspace,Minsup,Xvar,Yvar]])
  (= 
    (Candidate 
      (S $K) $LinkType $Dbspace $Minsup $Xvar $Yvar) 
    (let* 
      ( ($Prev 
          (if 
            (== $K Z) Z 
            (fromNumber 
              (- 
                (fromNat $K) 1)))) 
        ($Comb 
          (and 
            (get_pattern 
              (Candidate $K $LinkType $Dbspace $Minsup $Xvar $Yvar)) 
            (get_pattern 
              (Candidate $Prev $LinkType $Dbspace $Minsup $Xvar $Yvar))))) 
      (support $Comb $Dbspace $Minsup $Xvar $Yvar)))


;; Mine frequent patterns
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[miner,Dbspace,Minsup,Depth],[superpose,[[extract_val_set,Dbspace],[let,Link,[getlinks],['Candidate',Depth,Link,Dbspace,Minsup,Xvar,Yvar]]]])
  (= 
    (miner $Dbspace $Minsup $Depth) 
    (superpose 
      ( (extract_val_set $Dbspace) 
        (let $Link 
          (getlinks) 
          (Candidate $Depth $Link $Dbspace $Minsup $Xvar $Yvar)))))


;; Mine Surprising Patterns
  ; Action: load=metta_defn('&self',[surprisingMiner,Dbspace,Minsup,Depth,Highsurp],[let,Cptrn,[miner,Dbspace,Minsup,Depth],[superpose,[[getUniverseSize,Dbspace],[[let,Isurp,[isurprisingness,Cptrn,Dbspace],[if,[>,Isurp,Highsurp],[surp,Cptrn,Isurp],[nop]]]]]]])
  (= 
    (surprisingMiner $Dbspace $Minsup $Depth $Highsurp) 
    (let $Cptrn 
      (miner $Dbspace $Minsup $Depth)

        ( (getUniverseSize $Dbspace) 
          ( (let $Isurp

                (> $Isurp $Highsurp) 
                (surp $Cptrn $Isurp) 
                (nop))))))))
